" 'sheng kahati hai, 'maance, falon or subjiyon se sookshm jeevon ke khatme ke liye bhi dalacheenee ke tel kaa upyog kiya jaataa he, taaki ise lambey samay tak sangrakshit kiya ja sake

 coli) called' Shiga '

 turm 1 ke ejams main ab bas kuch hi din rah gaye hai
 In such a situation, if you want to bring good marks in maths, then these tips can be useful for you
 
 
 pariksha se pehle hone vaale tanaav se bachane kaa ye he sabase sahi tarika
 
 
 1
 un chaptars par najar zyada rakhen, jinase sabase zyada sawaal puche jate hai
 2
 pichley paanch saal ke queshchan paper solve karen
 This will give you an idea of what kind of questions are asked in the exam
 intervyuu main sabase zyada puche jate hai ye 8 sawaal3
 No matter how good the preparation is, Marx cannot come good unless you revise
 kyonki revijan ke dauraan hi kai douts clear hote hai
 4
 jo bhi padhein uskaa short nots banaate rahen
 When there is less time left in the examination, it will help in revision
 5
 Prepare for the subjects in which you are weak
 offis main jamaana he impresssont, to kaam aaenge ye tips6
 Examination does not mean that you keep studying all the time
 behatar hoga ki aap padhai ke bich thodaa vakt nikaalkar tivi dekhen, khelen, parivaar se baat aadi karen
 This will refresh your mind and you will be able to study well
